**Fetch Master-universe Data**
----
	Returns list of master-universe company's data in form of json for the specific portfolio object passed as input.
*   **URL:**
    /master-universe/fetch-investible-universe
*   **Method:**
    `POST`
*   **Path Params:**
    _None_
*   **Required:**
    * **requestBody:**
	```json
	{
	  "companies": [
		{
		  "amountInvested": 0,
		  "controversyScore": 0,
		  "environmentalFactors": [
			{
			  "name": "string",
			  "score": 0
			}
		  ],
		  "environmentalScore": 0,
		  "esgCombinedScore": 0,
		  "esgScore": 0,
		  "governanceFactors": [
			{
			  "name": "string",
			  "score": 0
			}
		  ],
		  "governenceScore": 0,
		  "holdingValue": 0,
		  "influenceESGCombinedScore": 0,
		  "influenceESGSCore": 0,
		  "influenceESGScoreForSustainalytics": 0,
		  "influenceEnvironmentalScore": 0,
		  "influenceEnvironmentalScoreForSustainalytics": 0,
		  "influenceGovernanceScore": 0,
		  "influenceGovernanceScoreForSustainalytics": 0,
		  "influenceSocialScore": 0,
		  "influenceSocialScoreForSustainalytics": 0,
		  "isOutlier": true,
		  "isin": "string",
		  "name": "string",
		  "outlierScore": 0,
		  "refinitivNormalisedScore": 0,
		  "socialFactors": [
			{
			  "name": "string",
			  "score": 0
			}
		  ],
		  "socialScore": 0,
		  "sustainalyticsTotalESGScore": 0,
		  "sustainalyticsTotalEnvironmentalScore": 0,
		  "sustainalyticsTotalGovernanceScore": 0,
		  "sustainalyticsTotalSocialScore": 0,
		  "sustainlyticsEnvironmentalScore": 0,
		  "sustainlyticsEsgScore": 0,
		  "sustainlyticsGovernenceScore": 0,
		  "sustainlyticsNormalisedScore": 0,
		  "sustainlyticsSocialScore": 0,
		  "totalESGCombinedScore": 0,
		  "totalESGScore": 0,
		  "totalEnvironmentalScore": 0,
		  "totalGovernanceScore": 0,
		  "totalSocialScore": 0,
		  "wt": 0
		}
	  ],
	  "contraversyScore": 0,
	  "countryAllocation": {
		"countryAllocation": {
		  "additionalProp1": 0,
		  "additionalProp2": 0,
		  "additionalProp3": 0
		}
	  },
	  "createdDate": "2021-02-09T13:59:39.717Z",
	  "currency": [
		"string"
	  ],
	  "currencyAllocation": {
		"currencyAllocation": {
		  "additionalProp1": 0,
		  "additionalProp2": 0,
		  "additionalProp3": 0
		}
	  },
	  "envScore": 0,
	  "environmentalFactors": [
		{
		  "name": "string",
		  "score": 0
		}
	  ],
	  "esgCombinedScore": 0,
	  "esgScore": 0,
	  "govScore": 0,
	  "governanceFactors": [
		{
		  "name": "string",
		  "score": 0
		}
	  ],
	  "investableUniverseFilter": {
		"environmental": 0,
		"esg": 0,
		"governance": 0,
		"selectedCountries": [
		  "string"
		],
		"selectedSectors": [
		  "string"
		],
		"social": 0
	  },
	  "investableUniverseType": "string",
	  "portfolioId": "string",
	  "portfolioName": "string",
	  "portfolioType": "string",
	  "portfolioUser": "string",

		"string"
	  ],
	  "sector": {
		"sectors": {
		  "additionalProp1": 0,
		  "additionalProp2": 0,
		  "additionalProp3": 0
		}
	  },
	  "socialFactors": [
		{
		  "name": "string",
		  "score": 0
		}
	  ],
	  "socialScore": 0,
	  "sustainalyticsCombinedScore": 0,
	  "sustainalyticsEnvScore": 0,
	  "sustainalyticsGovScore": 0,
	  "sustainalyticsSocialScore": 0
	}
	```
